A programming language composed entirely of whitespace. -
An overview of the Whitespace programming language, its unique features, and how it works.
Tool to decode / code in whitespace, an exotic programming language that only uses blank / invisible characters like space, tab or newline/line feed.
Whitespace is a fascinating esoteric language that flips traditional programming on its head, inverting the convention of meaningful characters and passive whitespace.
Interactive in-browser environments keep you engaged and test your progress as you go.

Whitespace is an esoteric programming language with syntax where only whitespace characters have meaning � contrasting typical languages that largely ignore whitespace characters.
